re-
NOTE ON USAGE ÓÃ·¨: In many verbs beginning with re- the prefix is pronounced / rI-; rI-/ or / re-; rZ-/ and it may have lost its original meaning of `again' or `back' ÔÚÒÔ re- ¿ªÊ¼µÄĞí¶à¶¯´ÊÖĞ, Õâ¸öÇ°×º¶Á×÷ / rI-; rI-/ »ò / re-; rZ-/, ²¢ÓĞ¿ÉÄÜÒÑÊ§È¥Ô­À´µÄ£àÔÙ¡¢ ÓÖ£§»ò£à»Ø£§µÈÒâÒå: / rI-; rI-/ recall, repair; / re-; rZ-/ represent. Other verbs have had re- added to them with the meaning of `again' and it is pronounced / ri:-; ri-/ ÁíÓĞÒ»Ğ©¶¯´Ê¼Ó re- ±íÊ¾£àÔÙ¡¢ ÓÖ£§Ö®Òâ, ¶Á×÷ /ri:-; ri/: reopen; recreate. There are a few verbs which fit into both groups and a hyphenmay be used to show the distinction »¹ÓĞÒ»Ğ©¶¯´ÊÊÊºÏì¶ÉÏÊöÁ½ÖÖÇé¿ö, ¿ÉÓÃÁ¬½ÓºÅ±íÊ¾ÕâÖÖÇø±ğ: recount / rI5kaUnt; rI`kaJnt/ = `tell a story', re-count / 9ri:5kaUnt;9ri`kaJnt/ = `count again'; recover / rI5kQvE(r); rI`kQvL/ = `get back' or `become well again', re-cover / 9ri:5kQvE(r);9ri`kQvL/ = `supply with a new cover'.

relation
NOTE ON USAGE ÓÃ·¨: Compare relation, relationsand relationship. ÊÔ±È½Ïrelation¡¢ relations¡¢ relationshipÕâÈı¸ö´Ê. Relationship has the widest use, covering many of the meanings of relation and relations. *relationshipÓÃ·¨×î¹ã, °üÀ¨ÁËrelationºÍrelationsµÄĞí¶àº¬Òå.  1 Relation and relationshipcan be used of family connections *relationºÍrelationship¿ÉÓÃÒÔ±íÊ¾Ç×Êô¹ØÏµ: A relation of mine is coming to stay. ÎÒÓĞ¸öÇ×ÆİÒªÀ´´ËÔİ×¡. *  `What's your relationship to her?' `She's my cousin.' £àÄã¸úËıÊÇÊ²÷áÇ×Æİ?£§£àËıÊÇÎÒµÄ±íÃÃ.£§  2 Relationship can indicate a strong emotional association *relationship¿ÉÒÔÖ¸Ç¿ÁÒµÄ¸ĞÇéÁªÏµ: Their relationship has lasted many years.
